[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root-Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability stems from reading the “tesseract-path” custom metadata [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue from the PDF [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mpdDocument.getDocumentInformation[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getCustomMetadataValue[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTESSERACT_PATH_KEY[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand passing it directly, without validation, as the program name in the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ProcessBuilder` command list. An attacker-controlled PDF can embed arbitrary [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent into that metadata entry, leading to arbitrary OS command execution.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Fix: Disable Untrusted Metadata Override[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove or disable the code that reads and honors the `tesseract-path` metadata[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mkey.[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Always use the internal `tesseractPath` field [0m[1;39m([0m[39minitialized to the trusted [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault `[0m[32m"tesseract"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when constructing the OCR command. This ensures that [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted PDF content cannot dictate which binary or script is executed.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Implementation Steps[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `[0m[1;35mOCRStreamEngine.runTesseract[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath image[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Delete [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor comment out[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m the block that fetches `actualTessPath` from PDF [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m158[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m163[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace with:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         String actualTessPath = this.tesseractPath;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Leave the remainder of `runTesseract` unchanged so that the image‐to‐text [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworkflow proceeds normally.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Clean up class members:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Remove the `TESSERACT_PATH_KEY` constant and any related Javadoc [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferencing a metadata override.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Update the class-level Javadoc to no longer mention metadata‐based [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Provide an API‐level override [0m[1;39m([0m[39moptional enhancement[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If end users require customizing the Tesseract executable path, introduce a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic setter on `OCRStreamEngine`:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        public void [0m[1;35msetTesseractPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m this.tesseractPath = path; [0m[1;39m}[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Document that this setter must be invoked programmatically [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot via PDF [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before calling `[0m[1;35mgetText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By eliminating the metadata override, we close the injection channel entirely:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ProcessBuilder` will only ever invoke an attacker‐controlled program name if the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication code itself has explicitly set it via the new setter API.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing logic for rendering pages, creating temp files, launching [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTesseract as a list‐based `ProcessBuilder` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthus avoiding shell interpolation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreading output remains intact.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness changes are required. Fuzzing continues to supply arbitrary PDFs, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut cannot inject OS commands.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - External dependencies, tests, and utilities are untouched. Only the single [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod for building the command is hardened.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Users who previously relied on embedding a custom Tesseract path in PDF [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata will lose that capability. Mitigation: offer the new [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msetTesseractPath[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` API and clearly document this change in release notes.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No performance or functional regressions are expected in standard use, as the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcalling `[0m[32m"tesseract"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is preserved.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Similar Patterns in Codebase[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other PDFBox components do not derive executable names from document metadata.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAligning `OCRStreamEngine` with that pattern enhances consistency and safety.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase was flagged by Jazzer as vulnerable to OS command injection when [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoking Tesseract in `OCRStreamEngine`. The fuzzer stack trace shows untrusted [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata flowing into `[0m[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. A patch was attempted that removed the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPDF metadata override for the Tesseract path, added a `[0m[1;35msetTesseractPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod, and forced use of the programmatic path only. Applying the patch produced a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation error: `[0m[1;35msetTesseractPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is already defined in the class, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreventing the build from succeeding.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer security sanitizer detected a critical OS command injection [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerability arises in `[0m[1;35mOCRStreamEngine.runTesseract[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` where the code [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads a custom metadata value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tesseract-path`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m from the PDF document and uses it [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min a `ProcessBuilder` invocation.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer stack trace:  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `OsCommandInjection.processImplStartHook`  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `ProcessBuilder.start`  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `OCRStreamEngine.doOCR` → `runTesseract` → `processPage` → `writeText` → [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PDFOCRFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code uses [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mpdDocument.getDocumentInformation[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getCustomMetadataValue[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"tesseract-path"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverride the default executable path.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No validation or sanitization is applied to the retrieved metadata string before [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassing it to `ProcessBuilder`.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The default `tesseractPath` field is “tesseract,” but can be overridden by [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker-controlled PDF metadata.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFOCRFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m drives this path by feeding arbitrary PDF inputs, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotentially embedding malicious metadata.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removed the static metadata key constant `TESSERACT_PATH_KEY`.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Deleted logic that fetched and applied the metadata override.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Introduced a public setter `[0m[1;35msetTesseractPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-null/non-empty check.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changed `runTesseract` to always use `this.tesseractPath`.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Compilation failed with a duplicate-method error:  [0m                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39morg.apache.pdfbox.ocr.OCRStreamEngine”  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The build log pinpoints the error in `OCRStreamEngine.java` at line [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m, [0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the change.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Eliminate Metadata-Based Path Override[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `private String [0m[1;35mrunTesseract[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath image[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, replace the logic that retrieves[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mgetCustomMetadataValue[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"tesseract-path"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with a simple assignment:  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `String actualTessPath = this.tesseractPath;`  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This change prevents any untrusted metadata from reaching `ProcessBuilder`.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserve OCR Functionality[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leave the `doOCR` invocation and command-list construction intact. They [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready work with a safe, validated `actualTessPath`.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure that `tesseractPath` defaults to `[0m[32m"tesseract"[0m[39m`, so existing behavior [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39musing system-installed Tesseract[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged unless overridden by API [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcallers via `setTesseractPath`.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Testing and Validation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run the full test suite to confirm no regressions in OCR functionality.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a targeted unit test [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif not already present[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that calls [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msetTesseractPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35msetTesseractPath[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to verify that invalid inputs [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare handled gracefully.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally, add a fuzz test variant that tries to set malicious tesseract [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths via the setter and confirms that they are rejected.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removing the duplicate setter directly addresses the compilation error.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Ignoring PDF metadata for the executable path eliminates the OS command injection[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause, as confirmed by the fuzzer stack trace.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Retaining and hardening the existing setter preserves legitimate use cases [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g.,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprogrammatic configuration in environments where Tesseract isn't on the PATH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout reintroducing vulnerabilities.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes are made to harness code, fuzzing logic, or external dependencies, in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompliance with project guidelines.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This patch strictly confines modifications to OCRStreamEngine, avoids broad [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception catches, and keeps the validated logic localized, minimizing potential [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mside-effects.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
